# 一步一步的创建你的角色

<body>
<div id="winchm_template_top">
<div id="winchm_template_button"><a href="$$unsavedpage1.htm" title="Previous topic"><img alt="Previous topic" border="0" id="winchm_template_prev" src="template2/btn_prev_n.gif"/></a><a href="$$unsavedpage2.htm" title="Next topic"><img alt="Next topic" border="0" id="winchm_template_next" src="template2/btn_next_n.gif"/></a></div>
<div id="winchm_template_navigation">Help &gt; 
规则部分 &gt; <a href="$$unsavedpage1.htm">建立人物卡来参与游戏</a> &gt; </div>
<div id="winchm_template_title">一步一步的创建你的角色</div>
</div>
<div id="winchm_template_container">
<div id="winchm_template_content">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">一步一步的创建你的角色卡：</font></span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">===========================================================================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">要参与无限流</font>TRPG<font face="宋体">游戏，作为角色而言，你的第一步是要创建一个属于自己的角色。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">在未来的游戏中，你需要以该角色作为你在游戏世界中的角色，与其他人或物进行互动，所以它将伴随你很长一段时间，请谨慎对待它，并在创建的时候想好自己将创造一个什么样的角色。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">你的角色由一堆游戏相关的数据，以及一些扮演要素组合而成，当然它的外貌体态也都由你决定，不过前提要符合游戏的规则。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">在创建开始之前，你可以先通过想象自己要扮演一个什么样的角色，是一个正义凌然的修道士，还是一个喜欢偷袭的刺客，又或者是一个勇敢无比的战士，还是一个扛着火箭炮的孤胆英雄。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">如果你没有什么自己的想法，则你可以大致翻阅一下本书的资源部分，看看有没有什么资源让你感兴趣。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">当你确定好自己要做一个什么角色的时候（一般我们称之为</font>“车卡”），就可以按照下述的步骤开始创造自己的角色了。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">你需要用笔或者纸（当然电子产品也可以）记录下来你要车的这张卡的相关数据，一来方便查阅，二来后续你也需要通过其来进行强化自身，毕竟这么多的数据是无法全靠脑子来记录的。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">而一张无限流</font>TRPG<font face="宋体">游戏的角色卡一般分为六个部分，分别为“概念段”，“属性段”，“技能段”，“专长段”，“衍生属性段”，“能力段”。下面将详细叙述除了“能力段”之外的每一段中的数据及数据的意义。</font></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">特殊：一般而言，一张新建的角色卡没有“能力段”，该部分是指人物进行了强化之后的特殊能力的列表，只有当角色强化特殊能力之后，才会拥有该部分。<o:p></o:p></font></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">===========================================================================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">概念段</font></span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">人物概念定义了人物的形象，背景，性格特征等扮演要素。我们取一张人物卡的概念段作为参考：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">姓名：罗兰</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">性別：男</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">年龄：</font>20</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">身高</font>/<font face="宋体">体重：</font><font face="Calibri">180cm/56kg</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">种族</font>/<font face="宋体">国籍：人类</font><font face="Calibri">/</font><font face="宋体">英国</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">外貌</font>/<font face="宋体">特征：金色的灿烂的长发</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">性格</font>/<font face="宋体">个性：总而言之，算是个滥好人吧。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">概述：我的父母给我起了古代圣骑士的名字。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">在很长的一段时间里，我都没有弄明白那个名字的含义。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">圣骑士什么的啊，真是距离我们的生活很遥远呐。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">远到</font>……<font face="宋体">有些遥不可及。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">但是平静的生活也没什么不好，我不讨厌这样的生活，甚至可以说是有点喜欢这样的生活，我的人生也许就是这样的东西那，平淡但又不失趣味。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">但是那一天的我，有点冲动了呐。（笑）</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">明明知道的，如果把炸弹从车上移走的话，肯定会死。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">但是身体还是没有受到自己的控制就动起来了。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">“</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">啊啊，我真的是啊。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">”</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">我这样的感慨到，拼近全力的朝着远方跑去。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">“</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">这种事情不该由我这样的平民区做啊。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">”</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">我一边跑一边哭着，但是却没有后悔，如果牺牲我一个可以拯救更多的话，那么牺牲了也无妨。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">至少最后一刻，我还是没有愧对自己的名字嘛。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">你需要自己为自己的卡起好名字，设定好性别，年龄，身高，体重等要素。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">这些相关的概念一般情况下请按照正常人类的标准。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">若没有特殊的能力，则一般情况下，普通的角色入场的时候都是人类，国籍可以按照自己的喜好和名字进行任意选择。当你后续因为某能力改变了自身的种族的时候，请不要忘记过来修改自己的种族。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">之后根据自己的国籍和种族以及身高体重来大致描绘一下自己的外貌特征。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">然后就是自己的背景了，你可以写一个身处英国的老北京，也可以写一个处于非洲落后地区的白人，只要符合上述的要求都可以。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">但是作为一个地地道道的老北京，你的父母祖上都是中国人，那么你自己一头靓丽的金发，名字叫做</font>“彼得”或者”碰碰小卡车”确实不太合适。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">===========================================================================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">属性段</font></span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">人物的属性定义了人物先天所具备的最为基本的能力。这些属性决定了角色在游戏中所能的事情。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">人物的属性一共分为九项，他们分别对应三大类属性：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">心智系属性</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">具体这些属性的功能以及作用请看</font>“属性概述”章节，这里只阐述如何创建角色时决定你的属性。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">首先，将人物的所有属性基本值设置为2</font>。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">将3</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点</font>/2</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点</font>/1</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点的点数</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">按照这自身意愿</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">任意分别分配给生理、心智、互动三类属性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">（你可以将3</font>点分配给生理系属性，也可以将这3点分配给心智系属性）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，然后将点数加在各项属性上。然后，将</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">6</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点自由点数任意加在想要提高的属性上。另外，将一项已经加到</font>4的属性提升到5，需要耗费2点点数</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，若没有特殊说明，则无法在建卡的时候将属性突破</font>5点</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">我们依然将</font>“罗兰”的人物卡作为参考：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">作为一名骑士，身体素质是不可或缺的。罗兰将3</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点属性点分配到生理属性上，2</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点分配到心智属性上，1</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点分配到了互动属性上。他将2</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点属性加到力量上，1</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点加到了耐力上；将1</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点属性加到了决心上，1</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">点属性加到了感知上，</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">然后将1</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点属性</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">加到了沉着上</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">。他的属性变成了这样：</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">力量</font> </span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">4</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">敏捷</font> 2</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">耐力</font> 
3 </span></i><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">智力</font> 2</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">感知</font> 3</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">决心</font> 3</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">风度</font> 2</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">操控</font> 2</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">沉着</font> 3</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">然后他将3</font>点自由属性分配给了耐力，</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">2点自由属性分配给了力量，1点自由属性分配给了敏捷，</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">完成了属性段的建卡。现在他的属性变成了这样：</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">力量</font> </span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">5</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">敏捷</font> </span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">3</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">耐力</font> </span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">5</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">智力</font> 2</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">感知</font> 3</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">决心</font> 3</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">风度</font> 2</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">操控</font> 2</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">沉着</font> 3</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">
</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">===========================================================================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">技能段</font></span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">人物的技能定义了人物后天学习所得的，做某件具体事情的能力和技巧。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">与属性一样，它分为三大类技能，也就是生理</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">系</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">技能，心智</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">系</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">技能，互动</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">系</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">技能。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">生理</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">系</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">技能：运动、肉搏、驾驶、枪械、手上功夫、隐藏、求生、白刃</font></span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">心智</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">系</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">技能：学识、电脑、手艺</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">（子分类）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">、调查、医学、神秘学、科学</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">互动</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">系</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">技能：动物沟通、感受、表达</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">（子分类）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">、胁迫、交际、掩饰</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">除了技能之外，每项技能下还细分无数个</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">“</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">专业</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">”</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">，表现以特定方式使用技能。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">“</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">专业</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">”</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">通常也由</font>ST<font face="宋体">和</font><font face="Calibri">PC</font><font face="宋体">协商决定，在</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">“技能概述”章节</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">中，我们列出了一些常用专业。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">当玩家在技能下拥有</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">对应</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">使用该</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">时，若</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">符合该专业的用法时会获得</font>1DP<font face="宋体">的专业加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri"><font face="宋体">特殊的是：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">手艺技能</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">并不是一项技能，而是一类技能的统称。手艺</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">——</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">和</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">手艺</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">——珠宝加工”</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">显然是两项完全不同的技能，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">首先，将人物的所有</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">技能</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">基本值设置为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">0</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">6</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点</font>/</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点</font>/</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点的点数</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">按照这自身意愿</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">任意分别分配给生理、心智、互动三类</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">技能（你可以将</font>6点分配给生理系技能，也可以将这6点分配给心智系）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，然后将点数加在各项</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">技能</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">上。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">然后，将</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">5</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">点自由点数任意加在想要提高的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">技能</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">上。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">另外，将一项已经加到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">3</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">技能</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">提升到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，需要耗费</font>2点点数</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，若没有特殊说明，则无法在建卡的时候将技能突破</font>4点</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">若拥有</font>“特殊身份1级”则技能将突破4点，</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">将一项已经加到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">技能</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">提升到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial">5</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">也</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">需要耗费</font>2点点数</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">另外，如同</font>“技能概述”所述，每个到达3级和4级的技能，都可以分别免费获得一个对应该技能的专业，同时，你还额外获得3个专业，但是这3个专业必须放在你至少拥有1级等级的技能上。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial"><font face="宋体">我们依然将</font>“罗兰”的人物卡作为参考：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">作为一名骑士怎么可能不会舞枪弄剑。罗兰将</font>6<font face="宋体">点技能点分配给了生理技能，</font><font face="Calibri">5</font><font face="宋体">点分配给了互动技能，</font><font face="Calibri">4</font><font face="宋体">点分配给了心智技能。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">接着，他将肉搏与白刃分别提升到</font>3<font face="宋体">级。将交际提升到</font><font face="Calibri">3</font><font face="宋体">级，将感受提升到</font><font face="Calibri">1</font><font face="宋体">级，在表达技能中选择了</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri">“演讲”</span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">子项，并且提升到了</font>1<font face="宋体">级。他把调查技能提升到了</font><font face="Calibri">3</font><font face="宋体">级，然后将神秘学技能提升到了</font><font face="Calibri">1</font><font face="宋体">级。</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><font face="宋体">现在他的技能列表是这样的：</font></span></i><i><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; FONT-STYLE: italic; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
